</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жность</a> (14924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожность.html>осторо́жность</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ostoróžnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predostoróžnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жностей</a></b>)

<ol><li>caution, precaution
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жности</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>predostoróžnosti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">out of caution</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принимать.html>принима́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ры</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:предосторожность.html>предосторо́жности</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prinimátʹ méry <b>predostoróžnosti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">take precautions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">предо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a> (10419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отвратить.html>отврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otvratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predotvratítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to avert, to stave off, to prevent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>войну́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvratítʹ</b> vojnú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to avert war</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасность.html>опа́сность</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvratítʹ</b> opásnostʹ (poražénije; krízis)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stave off danger (defeat; a crisis)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:агрессия.html>агре́ссию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvratítʹ</b> agréssiju/agrɛ́ssiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prevent aggression</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a> (27868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predotvratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predotvraščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to avert, to stave off, to prevent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>войну́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvraščátʹ</b> vojnú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to avert war</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасность.html>опа́сность</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvraščátʹ</b> opásnostʹ (poražénije; krízis)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stave off danger (defeat; a crisis)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращать.html>предотвраща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:агрессия.html>агре́ссию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predotvraščátʹ</b> agréssiju/agrɛ́ssiju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">prevent aggression</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***предотвращение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предотвращение.html>предотвраще́ние</a> (20457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предотвратить.html>предотврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predotvratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предписать.html>предписа́ть</a> (15358)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предписать.html>предписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predpisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предписывать.html>предпи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to prescribe</li>
<li>to direct, to order (+ dative + infinitive, someone to do something)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предполагать.html>предполага́ть</a> (2052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лага́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предпосылка.html>предпосы́лка</a> (11388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">предпосыла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predposylátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to precede (as an explanation)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предпосылка.html>предпосы́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predposýlka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предпосылка.html>предпосы́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предпосылка.html>предпосы́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предпосылка.html>предпосы́лок</a></b>)

</ul></li>
